)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******      - USE FINDFIELD SUBROUTINE                         AM
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******      - USE 1100/80 INSTRUCTIONS             AN

)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@!. ******* 3R1  - HANDLE ASCII AP
)@@G@@PRINT CONTROL IMAGES                   *******  @H@@@!. *******      - UAQ
)@@G@@PDATE TEST FACILITY                                *******  @H@@@!. ****AR
)@@G@@***      - USE BYTESUB 2R2                                     *******  AS
)@@G@@@H@@@!. *******      - GENERALIZE INPUT STRING LOGIC                    AT
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@!. *******      - ADD INPUT STRING VARIATIONS          AU
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@\. *******      - PROCESS ANY SDF FILE (EVEAV
)@@G@@N IF NOT PRINT FILE)       *******  @H@@@!. *******                     AW
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@!. ****************AX
)@@G@@**********************************************************  @E@@@!$(1),SAY
)@@G@@T   LIPROC$                     . INVOKE 'LI' PROCS   @E@@@!          TEAZ
)@@G@@P       A5,(1*/('Z'-'L')) . INIT 'L' OPTION KEY @ @@@!          S       BA
)@@G@@  A5,LOPT   @E@@@!          TEP       A5,(1*/('Z'-'R')) . INIT 'R' OPTIOBB
)@@G@@N KEY @ @@@!          S         A5,ROPT   @G@@@!          AN,U      A4,6BC
)@@G@@              . CALCULATE BATCH KEY = RUN TYPE-6@F@@@!          S       BD
)@@G@@  A4,BATCH          . BATCH=0 FOR BATCH RUN     @F@@@!          LMJ     BE
)@@G@@  X11,PREPF$        . PROCESS INPUT PARAMETERS  @C@@@!          ERR$    BF
)@@G@@                    . ERROR   @G@@@!          TEST                      BG
)@@G@@  . INVOKE TEST FACILITY IF @MASM,T @E@@@!          LMJ       X11,IDLINEBH
)@@G@@$       . GENERATE SIGN-ON    @C@@@!          PRINT$    IDBUFF,8        BI
)@@G@@  . PRINT IT@D@@@!          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   BJ
)@@G@@@G@@@!          L,U       X1,IMAGE          . INITILIAZE PTRS FOR STRINGBK
)@@G@@ INPUT@ @@@!          L,U       X2,HDBUFF @ @@@!          L         X3,(BL
)@@G@@1,0)  @E@@@!LOOP1     READ$     IMAGE,INIT        . READ NEXT STRING    BM
)@@G@@@D@@@!          L,U       A3,0,A0           . WORD COUNT    @ @@@!      BN
)@@G@@    LXI       A0,A3     @ @@@!          LXM,U     A0,IMAGE  @A@@@!      BO
)@@G@@    A         A0,(0100,0)     @ @@@!          TNZ       BATCH     @F@@@!BP
)@@G@@          PRINT$                      . ECHO INPUT STRING IF BATCH@G@@@!BQ
)@@G@@          MSI,U     A3,6              . CONVERT WORD COUNT TO BYTE COUNTBR
)@@G@@@G@@@!LOOP2     AN,U      A3,1              . CALCULATE ACTUAL BYTE COUNBS
)@@G@@T     @G@@@!          LXI       X1,A3             .   BY SUBTRACTING TRABT
)@@G@@ILING BLANKS@ @@@!          LMJ       X11,BGET  @ @@@!          TNE,U   BU
)@@G@@  A0,' '    @ @@@!          J         LOOP2     @G@@@!          L,U     BV
)@@G@@  A0,1,A3           . MOVE INPUT STRING TO HDBUFF     @^@@@!          LXBW
)@@G@@I,U     X1,0@ @@@!          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @G@@@!          S,S2    BX
)@@G@@  A0,HEAD,X3        . STORE BYTE COUNT IN HEAD TABLE  @E@@@!          L BY
)@@G@@        A1,X2             . GET STARTING BYTE # @ @@@!          SSL     BZ
)@@G@@  A1,18     @E@@@!          S,S1      A1,HEAD,*X3       . STORE IN HEAD CA
)@@G@@TABLE @F@@@!          A         A1,A0             . UPDATE HDBUFF POINTECB
)@@G@@R     @ @@@!          LXI       X2,A1     @F@@@!          INC       NHEACC
)@@G@@D             . INCREMENT HEAD TABLE COUNT@#@@@!          NOP     @E@@@!CD
)@@G@@          S         X2,X4             . SAVE HDBUFF PTR     @H@@@!      CE
)@@G@@    L,U       X2,ARROW          . SEARCH FOR AN ARROW IN INPUT (->)     CF
)@@G@@@ @@@!          L,U       A1,1,A3   @^@@@!          L,U       A2,2@A@@@!CG
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,FINDFIELD   @F@,@!          J         CONT0A    CH
)@@G@@        . NONE FOUND, NORMAL CASE   @F@@@,          J         CONT2     CI
)@@G@@        . NONE FOUND, NORMAL CASE   @G@@@!          TZ        A0        CJ
)@@G@@        . IS ARROW IN BEGINNING OF STRING?@B@,@!          J         CONTCK
)@@G@@0             . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT1             . NO@D@@@!CL
)@@G@@          L,T1      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . YES, GET SC,NC@I@@@!          A,CM
)@@G@@U       A0,0176           . INCREMENT SC BY 2 AND DECREMENT NC BY 2     CN
)@@G@@@F@@@!          S,T2      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . MOVE TO 2ND STRING DESCR  CO
)@@G@@@F@@@!          SZ,T1     HEAD-1,X3         . ZERO 1ST STRING DESCR     CP
)@@G@@@ @,@!          J         CONT0A    @ @@@,          J         CONT2     CQ
)@@G@@@G@,@!CONT0     S,S2      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . CHANGE BYTE COUNT FOR 1ST CR
)@@G@@STRING@G@@@,CONT1     S,S2      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . CHANGE BYTE COUNT FOCS
)@@G@@R 1ST STRING@F@@@!          TE,U      A3,1,A0           . IS ARROW AT ENCT
)@@G@@D OF STRING?@B@@@!          J         $+3               . NO@F@@@!      CU
)@@G@@    SNZ,T2    HEAD-1,X3         . SET 2ND STRING DESCR TO -0@ @,@!      CV
)@@G@@    J         CONT0A    @ @@@,          J         CONT2     @F@@@!      CW
)@@G@@    A,S1      A0,HEAD-1,X3      . GENERATE STRING 2 DESCR   @^@@@!      CX
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,2@A@@@!          S,S3      A0,HEAD-1,X3    @A@@@!      CY
)@@G@@    AN,S2     A3,HEAD-1,X3    @^@@@!          AN,U      A3,1@A@@@!      CZ
)@@G@@    S,S4      A3,HEAD-1,X3    @E@,@!CONT0A    L         X2,X4           DA
)@@G@@  . RESTORE HDBUFF PTR  @E@@@,CONT2     L         X2,X4             . REDB
)@@G@@STORE HDBUFF PTR  @F@@@!          J         LOOP1             . PROCESS DC
)@@G@@NEXT INPUT STRING @H@@@!INIT      L,U       A0,FCT            . INITIALIDD
)@@G@@ZE PRINT FILE FOR READING     @ @@@!          LXI,U     X11,PIRCB$@A@@@!DE
)@@G@@          LIJ       X11,BSDFIO$     @D@@@!          J         ERR2      DF
)@@G@@        . READ ERROR    @D@@@!          SZ        SWAP              . CLDG
)@@G@@EAR SWAP KEY@E@@@!LOOP3     L,U       A0,FCT            . READ NEXT SDF DH
)@@G@@IMAGE @ @@@!          LXI,U     X11,PIRCB$@ @@@!          LIJ       X11,DI
)@@G@@BSDFI$@D@@@!          J         ERR2              . READ ERROR    @D@@@!DJ
)@@G@@          J         END               . END OF SDF    @E@@@!          L DK
)@@G@@        A1,CONTROL        . GET CONTROL WORD    @F@@@!          JP      DL
)@@G@@  A1,DATA           . CHECK IF DATA CONTROL     @H@@@!          L,S1    DM
)@@G@@  A0,CONTROL        . NO, WHAT KIND OF SDF CONTROL IS IT?   @E@@@!      DN
)@@G@@    TE,U      A0,050            . IS IT SDF HEADER?   @B@,@!          J DO
)@@G@@        CONT1             . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT3           DP
)@@G@@  . NO@B@1@\          L         A0,(PF 1,NMESS4,MESS4)@G@\@!          L,DQ
)@@G@@H1      A0,CONTROL        . IS IMAGE THE SDF PRINT HEADER?  @G@@@\      DR
)@@G@@    L,H1      A1,CONTROL        . IS IMAGE THE SDF PRINT HEADER?  @A@\@!DS
)@@G@@          TE        A0,(0501125)    @A@1@\          TE        A1,(050112DT
)@@G@@5)    @A@@@1          TNE       A1,(0501125)    @^@@@1          J       DU
)@@G@@  $+4 @F@\@!          J         ERR1              . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEDV
)@@G@@ADER  @F@1@\          PRINT$                      . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEDW
)@@G@@ADER  @F@@@1          PRINT$    MESS4,NMESS4      . NO, NOT SDF PRINT HEDX
)@@G@@ADER  @ @@@1          J         LOOP3     @F@@@!          TNZ       LOPTDY
)@@G@@              . IF 'L' OPTION, PRINT LABEL@ @@@!          J         LOOPDZ
)@@G@@3     @H@@@!          PRINT$    LABEL,NLABEL,2    . 'PRINT FILE HAS FOLLEA
)@@G@@OWING LABEL ...'  @F@@@!          E$DIT     EPKT              . PRINT LAEB
)@@G@@BEL INFORMATION   @ @@@!          E$MSG     RUNID     @ @@@!          E$EC
)@@G@@FD1     IMAGE+3   @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG   ED
)@@G@@  USERID    @ @@@!          E$FD2     IMAGE+5   @^@@@!          E$SKIP  EE
)@@G@@  2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     PARTNO    @A@@@!          E$DECV    CONTEF
)@@G@@ROL,,S4     @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     INDEEG
)@@G@@V     @ @@@!          E$FD1     IMAGE+2   @^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   EH
)@@G@@@ @@@!          E$MSG     FILEN     @ @@@!          E$FD2     IMAGE     EI
)@@G@@@^@@@!          E$SKIP    2   @ @@@!          E$MSG     CREATE    @ @@@!EJ
)@@G@@          E$TIME    IMAGE+4   @^@@@!          E$SKIP    1   @ @@@!      EK
)@@G@@    E$DAY3    IMAGE+4   @D@@@!          E$PRINT   2                 . PREL
)@@G@@INT LABEL   @D@@@!          PRINT$    0,0,1             . SKIP A LINE   EM
)@@G@@@ @@@!          J         LOOP3     @D@,@!CONT1     TE,U      A0,060    EN
)@@G@@        . PRINT CONTROL?@D@@@,CONT3     TE,U      A0,060            . PREO
)@@G@@INT CONTROL?@ @@@!          J         LOOP3     @H@@@!          L,S2    EP
)@@G@@  A0,CONTROL        . GET # OF WDS IN PRINT CONTROL IMAGE   @H@@@!      EQ
)@@G@@    JZ        A0,LOOP3          . IF NO DATA, FIND NEXT CONTROL IMAGE   ER
)@@G@@@D@@@!          S         A0,NWDS           . SAVE # OF WDS @E@@@!      ES
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A0,6              . CONVERT TO CHARS    @C@@@!          S ET
)@@G@@        A0,NCHAR          . SAVE    @D@@@!          L,S6      X3,CONTROLEU
)@@G@@        . GET CODE TYPE @E@@@!          S,H1      X3,BASCII         . STEV
)@@G@@ORE FOR BYTESUB   @ @@@!          SZ        PRINT     @ @@@!          L,EW
)@@G@@U       X1,IMAGE  @ @@@!          L,U       X2,PRINT  @ @@@!          L EX
)@@G@@        R1,A0     @ @@@!          L,U       R2,12     @E@@@!          LMEY
)@@G@@J       X11,GETSFIELD     . GET NEXT SUBFIELD   @E@@@!          J       EZ
)@@G@@  LOOP3             . ALL BLANK, SKIP     @A@@@!          L         A0,(FA
)@@G@@'H@@@@@')   @F@@@!          TNE       A0,PRINT          . HEADING PRINT FB
)@@G@@CONTROL?    @C@,@!          J         CONT2             . YES     @C@@@,FC
)@@G@@          J         CONT4             . YES     @F@@@!          TNZ     FD
)@@G@@  KPRINT            . NO, IS PRINT KEY SET?     @C@@@!          J       FE
)@@G@@  LOOP3             . NO, SKIP@F@,@!          J         CONT5           FF
)@@G@@  . YES, SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL @F@@@,          J         CONT9           FG
)@@G@@  . YES, SUBMIT PRINT CONTROL @F@,@!CONT2     L         A0,(PF -0,0,0)  FH
)@@G@@  . WAS A REPORT JUST PRINTED?@F@@@,CONT4     L         A0,(PF -0,0,0)  FI
)@@G@@  . WAS A REPORT JUST PRINTED?@ @@@!          TZ        KPRINT    @E@@@!FJ
)@@G@@          PRINT$                      . YES, START NEW PAGE @E@@@!      FK
)@@G@@    SZ        KPRINT            . CLEAR PRINT KEY     @D@@@!          SZFL
)@@G@@        KHEAD             . CLEAR HEAD KEY@G@@@!          TNZ       LOPTFM
)@@G@@              . IF 'L' OPTION, PRINT HEADING    @ @,@!          J       FN
)@@G@@  CONT3     @ @@@,          J         CONT5     @^@@@!          SZ      FO
)@@G@@  A0  @ @@@!          LXI       A0,NWDS   @A@@@!          A         A0,(FP
)@@G@@0100,IMAGE) @ @@@!          EX        EPRINT,X3 @F@,@!CONT3     TZ      FQ
)@@G@@  PRINTALL          . IS PRINT ALL KEY SET?     @F@@@,CONT5     TZ      FR
)@@G@@  PRINTALL          . IS PRINT ALL KEY SET?     @F@@@!          J       FS
)@@G@@  MATCH             . YES, ALL HEADINGS MATCH   @H@@@!          L       FT
)@@G@@  X5,(1,0)          . COMPARE EACH INPUT HEADING TO IMAGE   @ @@@!      FU
)@@G@@    L,U       X2,HDBUFF @E@@@!LOOP4     TNZ       HEAD,X5           . SKFV
)@@G@@IP ZEROED HEADINGS@ @@@!          J         ELOOP4    @D@@@,          SPFW
)@@G@@1       KHEAD             . SET HEAD KEY  @G@@@!          TZ,S4     HEADFX
)@@G@@,X5           . NORMAL CASE (SINGLE HEADING)?   @B@,@!          J       FY
)@@G@@  CONT3A            . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT6             . NOFZ
)@@G@@@E@@@!          L,T1      A1,HEAD,X5        . YES, LOOK FOR MATCH @ @@@!GA
)@@G@@          LMJ       X10,SLIDE @F@@@!          J         ELOOP4          GB
)@@G@@  . NO MATCH, TRY NEXT HEADING@^@@@,          TNZ       ROPT@D@,@!      GC
)@@G@@    SP1       KPRINT            . SET PRINT KEY @D@,@!          SZ      GD
)@@G@@  HEAD,X5           . CLEAR ENTRY   @G@@@,          SZ        HEAD,X5   GE
)@@G@@        . CLEAR ENTRY IF NOT 'R' OPTION   @ @@@!          J         MATCGF
)@@G@@H     @D@,@!CONT3A    TZ,T1     HEAD,X5           . ->XXXX CASE?  @D@@@,GG
)@@G@@CONT6     TZ,T1     HEAD,X5           . ->XXXX CASE?  @B@,@!          J GH
)@@G@@        CONT3B            . NO@B@@@,          J         CONT7           GI
)@@G@@  . NO@E@,@!          SP1       KPRINT            . YES, SET PRINT KEY  GJ
)@@G@@@F@,@!          L,T2      A1,HEAD,X5        . LOOK FOR MATCH ON STRING 2GK
)@@G@@@G@@@,          L,T2      A1,HEAD,X5        . YES, LOOK FOR MATCH ON STRGL
)@@G@@ING 2 @ @@@!          LMJ       X10,SLIDE @F@@@!          J         MATCGM
)@@G@@H             . NO MATCH, KEEP PRINTING   @F@@@!          SZ        HEADGN
)@@G@@,X5           . MATCH FOUND, CLEAR ENTRY  @ @@@!          J         MATCGO
)@@G@@H     @E@,@!CONT3B    L,T1      A1,HEAD,X5        . COMPARE STRING 1    GP
)@@G@@@E@@@,CONT7     L,T1      A1,HEAD,X5        . COMPARE STRING 1    @ @@@!GQ
)@@G@@          LMJ       X10,SLIDE @F@@@!          J         ELOOP4          GR
)@@G@@  . NO MATCH, TRY NEXT HEADING@E@@@!          TZ,T2     HEAD,X5         GS

)@@G@@@B@@@,          J         CONT8             . NO@F@@@!          SP1     GU
)@@G@@  PRINTALL          . YES, SET PRINT ALL KEY    @D@@@!          SZ      GV
)@@G@@  HEAD,X5           . CLEAR ENTRY   @ @@@!          J         MATCH     GW
)@@G@@@G@,@!CONT3C    SP1       KPRINT            . XXX->YYY CASE, SET PRINT KGX
)@@G@@EY    @F@,@!          SZ,T1     HEAD,X5           . CLEAR STRING 1 PORTIGY
)@@G@@ON    @H@@@,CONT8     SZ,T1     HEAD,X5           . XXX->YYY CASE, CLEARGZ
)@@G@@ STRING 1 PORTION @ @@@!          J         MATCH     @F@@@!ELOOP4    TLHA
)@@G@@EM      X5,NHEAD          . ANY INPUT HEADINGS LEFT?  @E@@@!          J HB
)@@G@@        LOOP4             . YES, TRY NEXT ONE   @F@@@!          TNZ     HC
)@@G@@  ROPT              . IF 'R' OPTION, KEEP GOING @G@@@!          TZ      HD
)@@G@@  KHEAD             . WERE ANY HEADINGS ENCOUNTERED?  @F@@@!          J HE
)@@G@@        LOOP3             . NO MORE HEADS, NO MATCH   @F@@@!          J HF
)@@G@@        END               . NO, NOTHING MORE TO DO    @F@@@!MATCH     SPHG
)@@G@@1       KPRINT            . MATCH FOUND, SET PRINT KEY@E@@@!          TZHH

)@@G@@        CONT9             .   PRINT HEADING BEING PROCESSED @F@@@!      HK

)@@G@@    L         X2,(13,MESS3)   @ @@@!          L,S2      A0,HEAD,X5@ @@@!HM
